Canonical Verb Definitions\\n\\nThe authoritative list of allowed Kubernetes RBAC verbs (get, list, watch, create, update, patch, delete, deletecollection) is defined in multiple places:\\n\\n**a) Bootstrap Policy Verb Sets** (`plugin/pkg/auth/authorizer/rbac/bootstrappolicy/policy.go`)  \\nThe most semantically meaningful groupings used throughout the codebase:\\n- `Read = []string{\\\"get\\\", \\\"list\\\", \\\"watch\\\"}`\\n- `Write = []string{\\\"create\\\", \\\"update\\\", \\\"patch\\\", \\\"delete\\\", \\\"deletecollection\\\"}`\\n- `ReadWrite = []string{\\\"get\\\", \\\"list\\\", \\\"watch\\\", \\\"create\\\", \\\"update\\\", \\\"patch\\\", \\\"delete\\\", \\\"deletecollection\\\"}`\\n- `ReadUpdate = []string{\\\"get\\\", \\\"list\\\", \\\"watch\\\", \\\"update\\\", \\\"patch\\\"}`\\n\\n**b) FlowControl Validation** (`pkg/apis/flowcontrol/validation/validation.go`)  \\n`supportedVerbs = sets.NewString(\\\"get\\\", \\\"list\\\", \\\"create\\\", \\\"update\\\", \\\"delete\\\", \\\"deletecollection\\\", \\\"patch\\\", \\\"watch\\\", \\\"proxy\\\")`  \\nUsed to validate FlowSchema resource rules; any verb outside this set is rejected with a `field.NotSupported` error.\\n\\n**c) kubectl Role Creation** (`staging/src/k8s.io/kubectl/pkg/cmd/create/create_role.go`)  \\n`validResourceVerbs = []string{\\\"*\\\", \\\"get\\\", \\\"delete\\\", \\\"list\\\", \\\"create\\\", \\\"update\\\", \\\"patch\\\", \\\"watch\\\", \\\"proxy\\\", \\\"deletecollection\\\", \\\"use\\\", \\\"bind\\\", \\\"escalate\\\", \\\"impersonate\\\"}`  \\nUsed to warn users of non-standard verbs when creating Roles/ClusterRoles via kubectl.\\n\\n**d) kubectl can-i** (`staging/src/k8s.io/kubectl/pkg/cmd/auth/cani.go`)  \\n`resourceVerbs = sets.NewString(\\\"get\\\", \\\"list\\\", \\\"watch\\\", \\\"create\\\", \\\"update\\\", \\\"patch\\\", \\\"delete\\\", \\\"deletecollection\\\", \\\"use\\\", \\\"bind\\\", \\\"impersonate\\\", \\\"*\\\", \\\"approve\\\", \\\"sign\\\", \\\"escalate\\\", \\\"attest\\\")`  \\nUsed for client-side verb validation in authorization checks.\\n\\n**e) Code Generator** (`staging/src/k8s.io/code-generator/cmd/client-gen/generators/util/tags.go`)  \\n`SupportedVerbs = []string{\\\"create\\\", \\\"update\\\", \\\"updateStatus\\\", \\\"delete\\\", \\\"deleteCollection\\\", \\\"get\\\", \\\"list\\\", \\\"watch\\\", \\\"patch\\\", \\\"apply\\\", \\\"applyStatus\\\"}`  \\nDefines which verbs are supported for client-go code generation.\\n\\n### 2. HTTP-to-Verb Mapping\\n\\n**Installer** (`staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/endpoints/installer.go`)  \\n`toDiscoveryKubeVerb` maps HTTP methods to Kubernetes verbs for API discovery:\\n- DELETE → delete, DELETECOLLECTION → deletecollection, GET → get, LIST → list, PATCH → patch, POST → create, PUT → update, WATCH → watch\\n\\n**RequestInfo** (`staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/endpoints/request/requestinfo.go`)  \\n`NewRequestInfo` parses incoming HTTP requests and resolves the kube verb (including distinguishing list from get, deletecollection from delete). `verbsWithSelectors = sets.NewString(\\\"list\\\", \\\"watch\\\", \\\"deletecollection\\\")` identifies verbs that support field/label selectors.\\n\\n### 3. API Handler Enforcement\\n\\n**CRD Handler** (`staging/src/k8s.io/apiextensions-apiserver/pkg/apiserver/customresource_handler.go`)  \\nThe `serveResource` function dispatches on `requestInfo.Verb` with a switch statement covering all 8 standard verbs (get, list, watch, create, update, patch, delete, deletecollection). Unsupported verbs return a `MethodNotSupported` error.\\n\\n**API Installer** (`staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/endpoints/installer.go`)  \\n`registerResourceHandlers` maps each verb to its REST handler based on storage interface capability (Getter, Lister, Watcher, Creater, Updater, Patcher, Deleter, CollectionDeleter).\\n\\n**Delete Handler** (`staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/endpoints/handlers/delete.go`)  \\n`DeleteCollection` implements the deletecollection verb handler.\\n\\n### 4. Authorization Interface\\n\\n**Authorizer Interface** (`staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/authorization/authorizer/interfaces.go`)  \\n`GetVerb()` on `Attributes` returns the kube verb.
